| Wi d kra n yimedyaten n ṣṣenf n telɣa tudmawanin ay tezmer ad tent-id-tejmeɛ teṛmist-nneɣ ed wamek ay nezmer ad tent-nesseqdec. |
| Wid umi yura ad myussanen |  ad myussanen anect bɣun mbaɛaden. Wid umi ur yuri ad myussanen |  ur ttemyussanen ara ula ma mqabalen. |

| Yiwet n tnezzayt |  teffeɣ-d Cabḥa s afrag |  terra-tt tmara ad teqqim ɣer lqaɛa ɣef leblaḍ imi tḥulfa i yiman-is itezzi leɛqel-is. |

| Deg-s llan sḍis n srirat |  sḍis n tgidiwin |  sḍis n yisɣimen akked sḍis n texzanin anda ara srusun iselsa-nsen d tɣawsiwin-nniḍen. |

| Yal wa mlan-as axxam d wanda ara yaf srir-is iɣef ires wussu-s akked texzant-is anda ara iger iceṭṭiḍen-is d tɣawswin-nniḍen n wuɣus. |
| Ad teqqim ɣef tsumta yersen ɣef tqermet deg tesga |  ad tcennu tizlit deffir tayeḍ nettat ad tekkat abendayer |  tilawin ad cennunt yid-s. |
| Am tbuciḍant i yuzzel ɣur-s |  netta yettru |  yettɛeggiḍ s ṭṭelq n tgerjumt-is |  imeṭṭawen anect n lbunyat ttegruffuɛen-d seg taṭṭucin-is. |
| Beddlen tamagit s tayeḍ imi deg yiwen n umagrad-is teqqar-d : Zzayer d tamurt taɛrabt deg wayeḍ terna-d : Tineslemt d asɣan n uwanek . |
| D imjuhad udrigen |  mačči d wid irefden leslaḥ |  maca d nutni i ixeddmen akk timsal i yettarran amahil n umjahed iḍerru-d akken i iwata. |
| Deg wakud-nni |  tamdint ad d-teččaṛ d imdanen ara iɛerḍen ad awen-d-ssenzen tihyufin |  ad awen-akren tapizza-nwen neɣ ad ken-id-mmetren. |
| Ggran-d ala kra n yiḍan ay mazal sseglafen deg tegrawt tamẓerbeḍḍut. Mi asen-rran takmamt |  ad yens lḥess-nsen yernu ad nhenni seg-sen. |
| Imeḍqan n uḥraz n wuzzal akked yileẓwi ččuren |  dɣa |  Saɛid Usliman n Leɛzib n Zeɛmum yuzzel ad d-iheggi amḍiq-nniden beṛṛa n tkebbanit. |
| Init-d ay arraw-iw |  amzun tufa-tt-id tasa-w |  kra yekka wass d nettat tettefriwis |  nekk deɛɛuɣ s agellid ameqqran ad ffɣent deg telwit. |
| Lemmer maci d memmi-s n ubekkaḍ ay tellid |  tili mi ara tregmed yiwen |  ur d-tetteqqaled ara ad tessiwled yid-sen amzun acemma ur yelli. |
| Maɣef kan ur tettsemmid i tɣawsiwin s yismawen-nsent yerna ad testeɛṛfed tbeddel-ik s Umarikani-nni ay tessen deg uɣerbaz n tanglizit? |
| Maɣef kan ur tettsemmiḍ i tɣawsiwin s yismawen-nsent yerna ad testeɛṛfeḍ tbeddel-ik s Umarikani-nni ay tessen deg uɣerbaz n tanglizit? |
| Mi ara ɛeddin ad budden mmi-tsen neɣ yelli-tsen taqrurt qqaren-as: Ldi qemmu |  qmec ṭeṭṭu Ini gren-as taɣawsa-nni taẓidant deg yimi-is. |
| Mi d-yeḥḍer yimensi tessers-asent-d yiwen n lmetred iɛetter s seksu iseqqan s lmerqa n tɣeddiwt iwimi tger kra n tqeṭṭiḍin n tcedluḥt. |

| I teqbaylit tefka-m azal |  tsulim-as deg ccan |  tettcebbiḥem-aɣ ussan |  am yitran yettcebbiḥen igenwan |  neɣ am tziri yeḍwan |  deg wuḍan ɣezzifen. |
| Imẓerbeḍḍa zemren i lɛaṛ. Iḍelli d ibeɛtiyen ed yimeẓrislamen ay yellan nekkṛen tillin n tmaziɣt. Imir-a |  d imẓerbeḍḍa ay yeqqlen nekkṛen-tt. |

| Ɣas ma yella Tiziri tella tettini-iyi-d d nekk kan ay d argaz ara taɣ |  asmi ay as-nniɣ ma ad nezwej |  tenna-iyi-d UHU. Ur fhimeɣ acemma deg wanect-a. |
| Ay imdukal |  ay irfiqen-iw deg yir tiswiɛin |  wid yesɛeddan yid- kra qessiḥen d lmeḥna |  ad teẓrem belli ad d-neɛṛen igenwan ula ɣef tiyi ad tent-kfun. |
| D acu ay tebɣam? ay d-yesseqsa yemḍebber-nni ahendi. Nebɣa akk akal-a seg Tezgelt n Ugafa arma d Tizgelt n Wenẓul |  ay as-yenna ujiniṛal-nni anglizi. |
| Imẓerbeḍḍa d iremmaɣen. Iremmaɣen ḥemmlen ad ssiggden medden. S waya |  akken ad ḥebsen yiremmaɣen assigged-nsen |  yessefk d nekkni ara ten-yessiggden. |
| S tama-nniḍen |  tamurt-nneɣ tezga seg zik n zik ṭṭfen-tt yimhuras am Yifniqen |  Irumyen |  Ibiẓanṭiniyen |  Iwandaliyen |  Aɛraben |  Iṭerkiyen d yifransisen. |
| Sbedden-d yiwet n tsertit n uqader n tmeddurt tusligt ay yeqqnen ɣef wamek ara d-jemɛen |  ad sqedcen |  ad d-kecfen |  ad aznen neɣ ad ffren tilɣa-nwent. |
| Tamuɣli n yidir ɣef yidles-ines s umata temgarad mačči cwiṭ kan ɣef tin n wiyaḍ ig Rebbi d wid i t-iqerben cwiṭ deg uxemmem ɣef wamayendin n temsal. |
| Tennulfa-d Tkadimit Tazzayrit n Tutlayt Tamaziɣt. I yimẓerbeḍḍa d acu ara gen imir-a? Ad wten agejdur neɣ ad kksen ɛeryan |  ad gezren ikerbuben-nsen. |
| Tettwalid iman-nnem tgerrzed imi ala kemm ay yessawalen kraḍt n tutlayin gar yimeddukal-nnem? Ur ttaggad. Deg Tatoeba |  ur kem-nettwali ara tgerrzed. |
| Tiremt-a n tnezzayt d afenǧal ameqqran n lqahwa n uyekki ara isew userdas s tiḥdert n uɣrum yeḍlan s wudi akked ugumẓid  |  n lmecmac neɣ n tbexsisin. |
| Yiwet seg tnebdurin-inu timenyafin n Mark Twain d ta: Deg umennuɣ |  rrbeḥ ur yeqqin ara ɣer tiddi n uydi |  wanag ɣer tiddi yesɛa umennuɣ ɣer uydi-nni. |
| Cabḥa ur teṭṭif ara imeṭṭawen-is |  lehdur n temɣart-is sseḥlulin-d tasa-s |  tekker ɣer Nna Mennun tessudun deg-s nettat acḥal n awal i as-d-tessefruri. |
| Imdanen merra ttlalen-d d ilelliyen |  ɛedlen deg yiseɣ d izefan. Tettunefk-asen teɣẓint d tefrit |  yewwi-d fell-asen ad lḥun s tegmat deg way gar-asen. |
| Kra n yimẓerbeḍḍa qqlen ttaggaden ad d-kecfen tuqqna-nsen ɣer umussu amẓerbeḍḍu ladɣa seg wasmi ay d-iger uɣella n umussu-a tiɣri i urfad n yimrigen. |
| Tilawin ttheyyint iman-nsent akken i iwata akken ad d-fken udem yelhan sdat n yiɛeggalen n twacult ara yuɣalen sya ɣer sdat deg lehna d iḍulan-nsent. |
| Tizeɣwa n tɣuri akked tnuram zgant-d deg yiwen n uzaduɣ aɣezzfan n ukkuẓ n wannagen iqublen ilel |  llan diɣen kraḍ n yizaduɣen derren wa deffir wayeḍ. |
| Cabḥa ur teṭṭif ara imeṭṭawen-is |  lehdur n temɣart-is sseḥlulin-d tasa-s |  tekker ɣer Nna Mennun tessudun deg-s nettat acḥal n wawal i as-d-tessefruri. |
| Iḥun Rebbi ass-a mačči d suq |  ddeqs n yergazen ukk d yelmeẓyen i yellan di taddert begsen s tebɣest n sen sensen times tili ad tečč ura d ijufaṛ nneɣ. |
| Ilemẓiyen n tmurt n Leqbayen ɛebban-asen i yimariren n terbaɛt n Lezzayer semmus ɣer yilem deg temlilit taneggarut i d-yeḍran deg tlemmast n Lezzayer. |
| Kra n yimẓerbeḍḍa ttaggaden ad d-kecfen aseɣwen-nsen ɣer umussu amẓerbeḍḍu acku ttaggaden uguren ed teɣdemt. Yiwen seg-sen d unguf-nni ay iyi-iregmen. |
| Teddem-d taferkit-nni iɣef tura tabrat-is |  tettel-itt ɣef ukkuẓet n tikal |  tger-itt daxel n tjellabt n lkaɣeḍ teccemeɛ-itt |  terra-tt daxel n yiciwi-s. |
| Tikwal ma yella kra n umahil i tt-yeṭṭfen |  ma tberri ibawen neɣ tessirid iceṭṭiḍen neɣ tɛerrek taḥbult n uɣrum |  tcennu-d isefra iwimi tettarra aẓawan. |
| Yella-d uskasi ɣef ugama n Phaeton |  ay d-yenna Cooke. Yezmer ya ad yili d azunyur uqrib ɣer Wakal neɣ d asmil yeɣsin umi ttinin |  tikkal |  asmil n uẓru. |
| Zik |  zeṭṭent tuǧǧal tiqbayliyin iɛdilen akked yixellalen |  sakkin snuzunt-ten akken ad d-ssisent kra n uṣarif swayes ara d-aɣent iselsa i warraw-nsent. |
| Ad d-yemmekti kan ageɛmir-nni i as-d-ittebdaden yal iḍ deg tirga |  ad yettu akk ayen-nniḍen ala ayen iɣef t-id-iwelleh iɣef yecfa |  ur yezmir ad t-yettu. |
| Aṭas n tefyar ay d-yettwassuqqlen seg tanglizit ɣer yilsawen niḍen |  maca cwiṭ kan n tefyar ay d-yettwassuqqlen seg yilsawen niḍen ɣer tanglizit. Maɣef? |
| Ay akken nebɣu neqqen allen-nneɣ |  maca |  ur nezmir ad nezgel azal umezgun d wayen iga di yal tallit - ama di liser neɣ di ẓẓmek |  di talwit neɣ di ṭṭrad. |
| Imrabḍen ḥessben iman-nsen |  ttwalin iman-nsen d ihaggaren |  ssnen awal n Rebbi |  ifḍel-iten |  akka i ttwalin iman-nsen |  akka diɣen i ten-ttwalin Leqbayel. |
| Mi tuweḍ ɣer lemqam bu tqubbet isenden ɣef lǧedra n uẓebbuj awessur |  temlal din Dda ɛacur |  Werdiya |  snat yessi-s |  Zwina d Dehbiya akked kra n temɣarin. |
| Mraw |  snat n tmerwin |  kraḍt n tmerwin |  kuẓet n tmerwin |  semmuset n tmerwin |  sḍiset n tmerwin |  sat n tmerwin |  tamet n tmerwin |  tẓat n tmerwin |  tawinest. |
| S yiwet n tama wid akken i d-yedɛeq seg tmurt-is |  ad yethenni seg-sen |  s tama-nniḍen yebɣa ad yeẓẓu tutlayt taɛrabt akked tineslemt deg tmurt n Zzayer. |
| Ufiɣ yiwet n temdakelt tafransist di Lmerruk |  tenna-yi-d belli tudert n Paris mačči d tin n Fransa merra |  llant temdinin d tmennaḍin-iḍen cebḥent mliḥ. |
| Yuwi-tt ula ɣer Bgayet ad tt-twali yiwet n temsujjit d tamazzagt deg temsal n tarrawt |  maca ur tufiḍ s wacu i d-glant tirezzaf-a s waṭas s imesujjiyen. |
| Akken i t-id-yenna umaru Yusef Nacib : Aɛeddi seg timawit ɣer tira d ayen yeǧǧan tasekla tarusit |  tafransist |  taglizit |  taɛrabt d tespenyulit ad tnerni. |
| Ih |  akken d-teqqareḍ |  ula d nekk ad d-iniɣ : Ṭawes |  yelli-s n Si ɛellawa n At Ccurafa |  teqbel ad tezdi tudert-is d yiwen n Uqbayli iwimi ssawalen yidir. |
| Llant temnaḍin n tmurt n Leqbayel ideg mazal xeddmen tameɣra n tkerza |  qqaren-as daɣen tameɣra n yiweǧǧiben. Tameɣra-a xeddmen-tt ass amezwaru n tkerza. |
| Nemlal-d deg yiwet n teswiɛt ideg tuɣ teẓmek gar Marikan d imselmen - temẓmek ɣef lǧal n kra yiɣallen imazrayen ur neqqim kan deg uskasi asertan n tura. |
| Qqimen |  zzin-d i yiwet n tgida yersen deg yiwet n tesga |  heddren |  ttqessiren |  ttaḍsan |  ttemyeḥkun timseḍsa tineggura i slan deg taddart neɣ anda-nniḍen. |
| Tamɛayt meẓẓiyet |  tugar-itt tmacahut deg teɣzi |  tettfakka s yiwet n tenfalit taneggarut |  d nettat i d agmuḍ neɣ d tifrat n tuttriwin i nettaf deg uḍris. |
| Yal yiwen yesɛa daxel-is kra i t-iceɣben |  i t-iqerḥen |  i t-yesseɛyayen |  wa d targit |  wa d amenni |  wa d asmekti |  wa d kra n yiḥulfan |  yesseɣrasen ulawen. |
| Yerra-ten-id unemhal n uɣerbaz war isem ɣef kra n wumuɣen i isenṭeḍ ɣef yiwet n tfelwit iɛelqen ɣef uɣrab yellan sdat n temmurt n tudfa s abraḥ n likul. |
| Bab n tḥanut tecɣeb-it temsalt |  dɣa yedda ɣer Dima - ay yellan yettneffis s taẓeyt |  teccef-it tidi deg unyir - yernu yeqqim ɣef yifadden-nnes |  tama-nnes. |
| Dɣa ɣef waya i d-myezgen netta d yidir ɣas ma llan kra n yisekkilen yessemras Ufulkay mgaraden ɣef wid n Yidir |  maca aḥric ameqqran deg-sen kif kif-iten. |
| Irneggayen-nni imẓerbeḍḍa ay aɣ-d-yuznen iznan n tuggza ttun dakken |  ass-a |  tella temsulta tussnant ara ten-id-ijebden yernu ad ten-tezzuɣer ɣer tnefrut. |
| Llan kra deg-sen ssnen-t |  ssnen amek i iga |  ɣas ẓran d yiwen n urgaz ma yefka awal ur t-yettruẓu |  maɛna ḍemɛen ibeddel |  ɣef waya ɛeyyun deg-s ttḥellilen. |
| Nekkat tigusa deg yeɛrar-nneɣ axaṭeṛ |  xas yezwar ar tmes win yesɛan tabɣest |  tawaɣit-is mar ad yessiked nnig yiɣil-is |  ur d-ittttaf yiwen ad yeddu yid-s. |
| Segmi yebda iferreẓ timsal |  yeḥsa s yizerfan-is imezwura ttwarekḍen |  yekker ad yennaɣ s yimru |  yis-s yettaru ayen i t-iqerḥen yeqreḥ kra yellan am netta. |
| Wid yettcaxen di lawan-nni ɣullen Yidir d wid yellan am netta |  ur ten-seɣren ara deg tutlayt-sen |  seɣren-ten deg tutlayin tiberraniyin ɣef ugdud n tmurt. |
| Asmi ay lliɣ d ameẓyan |  lliɣ dima ttumareɣ armi d ayen kan deg yiḍ n wass aydeg ara neg tuffɣa taɣurbizt |  yernu ur iyi-d-yusi ara ula d nadam deg yiḍ-nni. |
| Di Tmurt-a |  mi ara tedduḍ di lebɣi i tmetti neɣ i twacult neɣ i yimdukal neɣ d ayen-niḍen |  ad tuɣaleḍ ad tettwaliḍ aberkan rnu ad d-teqqareḍ wa d amellal. |
| S wurrif d usḥissef d imeqqranen ara d-aruɣ imeslayen-a imi ur rjiɣ ara ad yettwagzem wawal-iw di Radio Tizi Ouzou di tedwilt n tsekla Wid ijebbden leqlam |
| Tetteffeɣ-d i tikkelt tamezwarut akken ad tissin iberdan |  tala |  tilawin n taddart imi ula d nettat akka d tasawent ad tuɣal d yiwwet n tɛeggalt gar-asent. |
| Win akken ay iɣilen yeḥkem |  atan yeẓẓel deg usenduq n wesɣar |  ur yettewliwil |  ma d wid ay d-yejja deffir-s |  mi ẓran yeqqel ur yenfiɛ i wacemma |  sserɣen-t. |
| Yessutur deg-sen ad as-d-fken ama d asefru n yimedyazen iqburen |  ama d anzi |  ama d timseɛreqt |  ama d kra n temɛayt yuklalen ad d-teqqim ur tettmettat ara. |
| Yuwey-iyi-d Ṛebbi kennemti ur tettwalimt iman-nwent d aḥric seg umaḍal. Ɣef leḥsab-nwent |  d amaḍal ay yellan d aḥric seg-went |  maca teccḍemt deg wanect-a. |
| Belɛid At Urejdal ɣur-s dderya d tamecṭuḥt |  lḥal iẓenner fell-as |  ilaq ad yinig ɣer tmurt n Fransa akken ad yessisi s wacu ara iɛeyyec arraw-is imeẓẓyanen. |
| Berra |  asemmid igezzem |  yesqaqar imdanen s yixxamen-nsen |  ad ẓẓiẓnen deg tesga ɣef yiri n ukanun |  times ur tettnus alama tɛedda tsemhuyt n ugris d qqajjar. |
| Ɣef tis sḍis n tnezzayt i d-mlalen akken ma llan yiɛeggalen imzazwaren |  Yidir |  Ṭawes |  Qadar |  Rabaḥ |  Sliman akked yinelmaden-nniḍen n uɣerbaz-nsen war isem. |
| Ma d yessetma-s |  teɛna-tent |  teṭṭef-itent-id i snat yid-sent ɣef tikkelt |  tessers aqerruy-is ɣef tuyat n Nnana-s Zwina |  teḍsa-d cwiṭ tuɣal tettru yid-sent. |
| Mazal yuɛer lḥal mliḥ akken ad d-yaf yiwen axeddim. Yerna ɣas txeddmeḍ |  rennun-d kan wuguren n wayen i ilaq ad txellṣeḍ |  si lqeḍyan n tḥanut alamma d lgaz. |
| Turart i bɣun uraren-tt maca ur ilaq ara ad ɣeflen |  ad ǧǧen biccuḥ |  akken i as-qqaren yigerdan i wuccen |  ad ten-yessxixxed seg yiwen neɣ n sin n yizamaren. |
| Yemma-m tesselmed-am aniwel d uqerdec n taduṭ maca tettu ur am-d-tenni ara d acu i yuɣen tameṭṭut ireclen mi ara yettezzi leɛqel-is |  tettemɛuqqu |  tettarra. |
| Yiwen ur yezmir ad aɣ-yegzem iẓuran lqayen |  i d-neggin d ayefki n teqbaylit i aɣ-yessuṭṭḍen! Yeqqar yinzi: Ay aman ur d-tugim yemma |  ur kkisen fad a tarwa. |
| Amur ameqran seg yigensaten |  gar-asen ula d atiliskud allunan n Hubble |  ḥebbun deg uḥbu aneddi n Wakal |  kra kan n timaḍ n yikilumitren nnig tjumma n tegnit. |
| Deg tiddi d aɛlayan am wakk atmaten-is |  tafekka-s rqiqet |  udem-is d aras |  leḥwal n uqadum-is akken ma llan qmumsen |  ur meqqrit ur meẓẓiyit |  d ilemmasen kan. |
| Efk-as-d asteqsi ɣef yisem n tmanaɣt n tmurt i tebɣiḍ deg umaḍal |  ad t-id-yaf neɣ ma yebda lehdur ɣef umezruy |  ladɣa win n Yimaziɣen |  ur t-tḥebbseḍ ara akk. |
| Imdanen ass-a ttazzalen deffir udrim |  leḥḥun ɣef yiɛebbaḍ-nsen am yizerman |  almi uɣalen ula d nnif |  tirrugza |  d yiseɣ ttnuzun ! cwi kan ddunit-agi d lfani ! |
| Qqlen yimẓerbeḍḍa am yiremmaɣen n Tegrawt Tislamant Tumrigt |  ttaznen iznan n tuggza i yimdanen ay yettmahalen deg unrar adelsan imi kan ur ddin ara yid-sen. |
| Qqlen yimẓerbeḍḍa |  ladɣa wid seg-sen ay yesɛan amahil yelhan deg Lezzayer |  ttaggaden ad ẓren wid ay d-yezzin fell-asen dakken ttekkan deg umussu amẓerbeḍḍu. |
| Turart i bɣun uraren-tt maca ur ilaq ara ad ɣeflen |  ad ǧǧen biccuḥ |  akken i as-qqaren yigerdan i wuccen |  ad ten-yesxixxed seg yiwen neɣ seg sin n yizamaren. |
| Ẓran akk medden dakken imẓerbeḍḍa nnummen ggaren-d tiɣri i utɛeddi ɣef wid ay yugin tiktiwin-nsen am wakken ay ttaznen iznan n tuggza s tekriḍt ed tmenɣiwt. |
| Akka i yenna wuccen ɣef tyuzaḍ mi ur yessaweḍ ara ad yekcem s akantu-nsent: Akka wala ad ṭṭsent |  netta yessenhaz war aḥbas tabeḥlust-is yesɛedda ddaw lmecbuk |
| Inelmaden n uswir wis kraḍ uraren-d yiwet n tnezgumt s teqbaylit |  d ayen iwimi yeɛǧeb i waṭas n yinebgawen imi ur nnumen ara ttwalin aya deg yiɣerbazen-nneɣ. |
| Mi iḥulfa yekkes-as ɛeyyu yerna yuɣal-d ɣer yiman-is |  yuɣal yebra-as lxuf-nni i t-irekben deg wasif-nni |  yekker ɣef yiman-is yuwi abrid n tuɣalin s axxam-is. |
| Nniɣ-ak-d ayagi acku tɣaḍeḍ-iyi |  teɣriḍ |  tḥedqeḍ |  tfehmeḍ |  yerna meẓẓiyeḍ |  tura kan i d-tbaneḍ ɣer ddunit |  widak-nwen a k-nɣen s tin n tismin acku tifeḍ-ten. |
| Tenna-as: Twalaḍ tura a Mhend Uccen yessuter-d deg-i yizem ad as-fkeɣ aqerruy-iw ad t-yečč maɛna ad iyi-d-yefk s lǧiha-s lgelba n temẓin |  yerna yegull-iyi-d. |
| Yemsegraw-d ugdud d ameqran n Yimarikaniyen beṛṛa i Uxxam Amellal akken ad sfuglen tamettant n yiwen n umdan akken ara sfuglen rrbeḥ deg temlilit n tcirḍart. |
| D lewqat igerrzen i d-sɛeddaɣ deg At Wizgan akked yimeɣriyen d yimdukal i d-yerzan ɣer temlilit |  anda i d-nuwi awal ɣef wungal-iw Asebbaɣ |  ɣef tsekla s umata. |
| Isegbaren d inaẓuren d imeẓẓawanen akked imyura zemren ad ssqedcen talɣiwin yemgaraden ideg llan wawalen yettwannan neɣ yuran |  tigawin |  tiɣmiwin akked leṣwat. |
| Maɛna taneslit amzun tḥeffu |  tetteqẓuẓur |  teḥḍem |  tettefruruy |  ahat ala yiwen nuẓar i d-yeggran yeṭṭef tarwiḥt ur tessuhel ara anda akken urǧin yuɣal-d yiwen. |
| Nečča-d iskilen d yifecka ɣer Dda Muḥend Ubelqasem s usafer n yimseɣti |  sakin Tiɛiwinin yedduklen d Teqbaylit |  wwin-aɣ-id tarbut n seksu s tmellalin tuftilin. |
| Turart urar |  ha-tt-an sdat-k |  maɛna ḥader ad iɛeddi fell-ak uzaylal |  ad teggriḍ deg nndama tameqqrant |  d acu n wudem ara t-tsekneḍ i yimawlan-ik d taddart-ik. |
| Anda tellid a amẓerbeḍḍu n lɛaṛ? Ṛjiɣ-k deg Tizi Uzzu |  amar ad k-waliɣ telsid-d taqendurt n weltma-k |  ad tceḍḥed cwiṭ |  i lmend n Yennayer |  maca ur k-walaɣ ara. |
| Imdanen i wumi yefka Rebbi tazmert |  tuwi-d fell-asen ad dlun |  ad rzun ɣer wid yuḍnen akken ad asen-kksen leɣben i d-yeɣlin fell-asen mi ten-teǧǧa tezmert-nsen. |
| Imi yella yeqqar deg Bumerdes ur neggug ara aṭas ɣef Tzerrajt |  ɣas yeqqim-n din ddaw n wayyur |  yemma-s yeḥsab-as Rebbi tettɣimi ur t-tettwali ara azal n lqern. |
| D tidet iɣallen usligen zemren ad ɛettben yerna ad nɣen imdanen ilemriyen? Iɣallin usligen sselkamen kan lameṛ. Sseqdacen-ten i lecɣal usligen |  akken bɣun ilin. |
| Di tallit-nni ddeqs n tesɣunin tidelsanin i irefden tutlayt n tmaziɣt ama s tira s yisekkilen n tifinaɣ ama s wid n tlaṭinit |  maca ttruḥunt s tuffra |  ddaw ufus. |
| Taglisya-nni zzat n wacu i d-nɛedda |  terna xemsa n ddqayeq kan terregreg ɣef lǧal n yiwet n zznezla meqqren |  dɣa nnig n meyya n imeẓẓulla i imeḍlen akken ddren. |
| Wissen ɣef teftist n yilel Agrakal deg Tici neɣ deg Tegzirt neɣ deg udrar maḍi anda mazal tasmuḍi teqqim-d ur tesuhel ara ɣas ma deg tlemmast n ssmayem i nella. |
| Yemm-as Mennun imi tettliwi tislit-is Cabḥa yellan s tadist am tmeṭṭut-is |  tezmer ad tkemmel lxir-is |  ad asent-tzeg i snat imi ttunaḥsaben i snat d tislatin-is. |
| Aɣerbaz n tmurt n Zzayer yewwet s uqadum ass-nni akken i t-ɛerben mačči s yiselmaden kan n tmurt maca s wid n tmura taɛrabin |  aḥric ameqqran deg-sen d Imasriyen. |
| Ɣas ma yella d nettat i yettnawalen |  i d-idhan d uxxam akk d tnebgawin |  Cabḥa |  kra ur as-iruḥ ɣef uheyyi n uẓeṭṭa |  telmed acḥal d taɣawsa ɣer temɣarin n lbaraka. |
| Tawilayt tis tlata deg umgerru uslulli : nniqal Tamurt n yiqbaylien ad tt-bḍun ɣer snat |  agzen ad t-snetḍen ɣer Zzayer Tamanaɣt |  azgen ad t-snetḍen ɣer Qsenṭina. |
| Tayemmat tḥemmel arraw-is ugar n yiman-is |  ur tettet almi rwan |  ur tetteṭṭes almi tettkel ur ten-ixuss kra. D nettat i d tigejdit n uxxam |  ma ulac-itt |  ad yeɣli. |

| Tilɣa ay nezmer ad tent-id-nejmeɛ fell-ak yezmer ad yili gar-asent yisem-nnek |  tansa-nnek n wemyaru |  uḍḍun-nnek n usawal |  tansa-nnek taliktṛunant |  wid ay tḥemmleḍ ad ten-tnermseḍ akked telɣa ay yeqqnen ɣer tkarḍa-nnek n wesmad. |
| D ayen ara ɛerḍeɣ ad geɣ - amek kan ara qqareɣ tidet akken zemreɣ |  s lekyasa zzat wayen i ɣ-yettrajun d axeddim |  imi tḥeqqeɣ dayen kan belli ayen i ɣ-icerken d ṣṣalḥa nekni s yimedanen yeǧhed s waṭas ɣef ayen i ibeṭṭun gar-aneɣ. |

| Kra n yirneggayen imẓerbeḍḍa ur ẓrin ara dakken Lezzayer tesɛa imtawayen n unmireg aɣedman ed Fṛansa ed Kanada yernu ibugaṭuten-nsen ulac d acu ay zemren ad asen-gen lemmer ad yeccetki fell-asen yiwen ɣef yigiten-nsen ijrimanen. |
| Lmut d ayen yezgan itekkes-aɣ lebɣi deg umeslay neɣ ula deg uxemmem |  maca tura faqeɣ belli win yeswejden iman-is i lmut d kra seg ayen i yezmer ad yeg ara s-yefken ugar akk n tmasit. Ma nmeyyeza-s i lmut |  ad tbin ad tudert-nneɣ. |
| Ad yekkat wul-is |  amzun yebɣa ad d-yeffeɣ |  ad tettergigi tɛeddist-is |  maca ad iɛeddi kan cwiṭ n wakud |  ad yuɣal akken yella |  ad as-yekkes cwiṭ cwiṭ lxuf-nni yugad |  ad yemlek leɛqel-is |  imir-nni timsal ad tent-yefreẓ akken i ilaq. |
| Ɣilen yimẓerbeḍḍa dakken zemren ad iyi-ssiggden s yiznan-nsen n tuggza. Tamezwarut |  ur ḥebbseɣ ara taḥemla-inu. Tis snat |  wid ay d-yuznen iznan-nni nessen-iten yernu ad ten-tessencew teɣdemt |  ad qqlen am tyuzaḍ-nni yuḍnen ajeǧǧiḍ. |
| Iserdasen-nni ubẓen-t |  qqnen-as tiṭṭawin-nnes |  sakkin uwyen-t ɣer deffir n tkeṛṛust-nsen. Yiwen seg yiserdasen-nni iḥukeṛ-it |  sakkin iqerres fell-as s aḍar. Asayes-a yettwaṣewwer-d yerna d imelyunen n medden ay t-yeẓran deg umaḍal. |
| Am twacult n At Umalu |  ula d nutni |  nettat |  yemma-s akked baba-s heyyan-d iman-nsen ad streḥben s yinebgawen ara yuɣalen qḍeɛ ccekk d iḍulan-nsen akka d tasawent imi Si ɛelawa |  igzem-it di rray |  yeqbel yelli-s Ṭawes |  ad tt-yaɣ Yidir. |
| Iwunak Yeddukklen rwin |  ɛerḍen ad rwin yerna mazal-iten ɛerrḍen ad rwin aṭas n tmura |  gar-asent Kuba |  Venezuela |  Colombia |  Ṣumalya |  Serbya |  Lɛiraq |  Iṛan |  Surya |  Afɣanistan |  Vietnam |  Birmanya |  Kurya n Ugafa |  Pakistan |  Rusya ed Ccinwa. |
| Uran-aɣ-d kra n waggagen iqbayliyen izzayriyen |  nnan-aɣ-d dakken gan tidiwenniyin ed yisemlen imẓerbeḍḍa sakkin nedmen. Nenna-asen ad arun i yimḍebbren n yisemlen-nni yernu ad asen-ssutren ad kksen tidiwenniyin-nsen seg yisemlen-nni. |
| Tikwal qqareɣ-as acimi ur iyi-d-yefki ara Rebbi d taqcict |  ad iyi-d-yernu kan cwiṭ n thuski am kemm a Ṭawes |  akken ad afeɣ win iwimi ara ɛeǧbeɣ |  ad iyi-yaɣ |  ur ttɣimiɣ ara deg uxxam n baba ad bureɣ |  ad xeddmeɣ ɣef tlawin n watmaten-iw. |
| Iserdasen-nni uwyen ilemẓiyen-nni ɣer yiwen n wemkan aydeg ɣilen yiwen ur ten-yettwali |  sakkin ddmen iẓra yerna bdan kkaten ilemẓiyen-nni s iɣef akked ifassen akken ad asen-rẓen iɣsan-nsen. Ur ẓrin yella win ay yellan yettṣewwir-iten-id. |
| Mi ara d-iniɣ tissist-a ur tettḍurru |  ur d-qsideɣ tzemred ad tt-teḍḍfed s yifassen-nnek yerna ad turared yes-s akken ay ak-yehwa. Tissisin timeqranin ur ttemmɣent ɣef yemdanen ala ma uwḍen-tent |  yerna ur yessefk ad tent-neḥseb d ilellac. |
| Tarbaɛt n yimeddukal i igan asniles-nsen s wul-nsen |  yeffeɣ leɛtab-nsen ɣer tafat imi uwin-d akayad-nsen akken ma llan yerna s tezmilin yelhan neɣ igerrzen |  ladɣa amusnak Sliman i d-yufraren d amezwaru gar merra inelmaden n wasun n Uqbu. |
| Iqerreb-d ɣur-i yiwen n userdas ad i wali d acu i d-nɛebba |  rriḥa-nni n teberra d yimurruten n uɣyul tewwet-it s anzaren-is |  terra-t ɣer deffir s sin neɣ kraḍ n yisurifen |  netta yettwaǧab s tefransist i uɣella-ines: Ttfuḥun-d warbaɛ-nni . |
| Titekniyin-nni n uɛetteb ay sqedcen Yimarikaniyen deg Afɣanistan |  Lɛiraq |  Guantanamo ed leḥbas uffiren niḍen snufant-tent-id yerna sqedcent-tent yagi tmura niḍen uqbel. Maca Iwunak Yeddukklen |  ɣef wakken ay d-yettban |  ɛerḍen ad tent-snernin. |
| Imeddukal i d-yuwin yiwen n umecwar aɣurbiz d Yidir d Qadar d Rabaḥ i izedɣen deg taddart n Yiɣil |  Sliman am Yidir deg Tewrirt |  ma d Ṭawes |  nettat n Tzerrajt anda akka yella uɣerbaz-nsen alemmas war isem imi ala netta i yellan deg tallit-nni. |
| Lemmer ad tesqedced neɣ ad twalid imeẓla ay itteg udeg-nneɣ neɣ taṛmist-nneɣ |  ama d imeẓla n baṭel neɣ d imeẓla s lexlaṣ |  ama d wid ay yeḥwajen ad d-tesnulfud amiḍan neɣ uhu |  yessefk fell-ak ad tɛahded ad tqadred tiwtilin-a timuta n usseqdec. |
| Tikwal ma yella yiwen |  iɣleb-it lḥal |  ur yezmir ara ad ibudd lǧar-is |  ladɣa ma d win yesɛan tin yellan s tadist deg uxxam-is |  mi ara iɛeddi ad d-iseww aksum i twacult-is |  ur ilaq ara tariḥt n uknaf n uksum ad taweḍ s anzaren n tin yettiniten. |
| Tanuḍt-nni yusmen ɣef lecɣal n tin isbedden aẓeṭṭa |  mi ara d-tebru i tyuga n yizgaren tettanef-asen ad alin ɣer tɣerɣert ad d-sukken acciwen-nsen seg uẓeṭṭa ara d-sɣersen ɣer lqaɛa |  yuɣ lḥal llal-is ulac-itt din |  ahat truḥ ɣer tala ad d-tagem. |
| Iwennaten gelmen-d ṣṣut-nni ujewwaq vuvuzella d akken yesseɛyaw |  d imciṭen |  qurenen-t dɣa ɣer tqeḍɛit n yilwen yeṭṭef yisiḍ |  ɣer terẓaẓayt n yibẓaẓ |  taɣaṭ iteddun ɣer tzelli |  taɣrast tageɛmirt yeččuren d tizizwa yessḍen neɣ abṛik yeččan lehyuf. |
| Akka |  seg zzman n zzman akka ay d nekkni |  ma telliḍ seg wid yettsetḥin |  ma telliḍ d anifi |  d uḥdiq |  ma tugiḍ lbaṭel |  ma tenniḍ tidet qerriḥen |  ma telliḍ d bab n tmussni |  atmaten-ik ad ak-rren deg rrif |  ad-ik-id-jaben ticrurin akken ad ak-ɣeḍlen. |
| Maca teẓriḍ |  mer ad d-nejmeɛ akk tifyar-a u ad tent-neǧǧ kan i yiman-nneɣ d ayen yesseḥzanen |  acku llant aṭas n tɣawsiwin i yezmer ad tent-yexdem yiwen yis-sent. Ɣef waya |  Tatoeba yeldi. Angal-nneɣ n uɣbalu yeldi. Isefka-nneɣ ldint i medden akk. |
| Neẓra dakken tagrawt tamẓerbeḍḍut la tetteg yiwet n tḥemla n ucemmet n kra n yimdanen ay yexḍan tagrawt-a yernu tamsalt-a ad taweḍ ɣer teɣdemt anda ara xnunsen aṭas seg wayt tegrawt-a deg waluḍ. Nesɛa akk inzaten ay yessefken i ubeddu n tsestant. |
| Acḥal n waklan ay teḥwajem ad ten-tawyem seg Tefriqt? ay d-yesseqsa yemḍebber-nni afriqi. Kra n win ay yesɛan ugar n mraw n yiseggasen |  yerna yezdeɣ deg tefsirt tutrimt n Tefriqt |  seg Meṛṛuk arma d Tafriqt n Wenẓul |  ay as-d-yerra uqebṭan-nni apuṛtugali. |
| Ass-nni akken i d-yeɣra Yidir i yinelmaden n tneɣrit-nsen aḍris n tmacahut Adrar aberkan  |  mi akken i d-ffɣen s abraḥ ad sgunfun neɣ ma uwin-d yid-sen kra ad t-ččen d tanalt |  yeqqim deg yiwet n teɣmert |  i t-id-yeɛnan d Tawes i as-yennan : Azul a Yidir ! |
| Awyet akk akal ay awen-yehwan. Ad yili dima wakal ara d-ikafin ama i yimellalen |  ama i Yihendiyen n Temrikt |  ay d-yenna yemḍebber-nni n Yihendiyen. D tidet? Ihi nekkni nebɣa akk akal ay yellan gar Ugaraw Aṛkti ed Ugaraw Antaṛkti |  ay d-yenna ujiniṛal-nni. |
| Awyet akk akal ay awen-yehwan |  ay d-yenna yemḍebber-nni n yiserwen. Awah |  ay as-yenna ujiniṛal-nni anglizi |  nekkni ad nawey kan yiwet n tegzirt. D acu-tt tegzirt-a? ay d-yesseqsa yemḍebber-nni. D tigzirt kan n Ustṛalya |  ay as-d-yerra ujiniṛal-nni anglizi. |
| Iẓeḍwan n tmussniwin ay sɛan yimeɣnasen n tmaziɣt meɣɣrit s waṭas ɣef wid ay sɛan yibeṛhac n yimẓerbeḍḍa. S waya |  imẓerbeḍḍa zemren ad ttwaɛezlen am uxunnis n yiẓẓan deg tmetti akken ma tella lemmer ad bɣun ad ḍurren ayen ay d-iḥeṛṛ Umussu Adelsan Amaziɣ. |
| Tagrawt tamẓerbeḍḍut ur tettwassen ara deg temnaḍt-nneɣ |  ur tesɛi ara din tiɣɣerfi |  ur teẓẓi ara deg-s |  yernu tiktiwin-nnes ur tent-ḍfiren ara medden din. S waya |  ur ẓriɣ ara maɣef ay mazal ḍemɛen yimẓerbeḍḍa dakken ad ssiwḍen ad gen kra deg temnaḍt-nneɣ. |
| Imaslaḍen n teɣlamt llan ttcetkin-d ɣef Christophe Colomb ay yellan yessaẓay taɣuni s uwifi n uɣerrabu s wuraren n Internet |  maca netta yenkeṛ arday-a s wurfan yernu yenna-d dakken la yesseqdac taɣuni akken ad d-inadi ikalen ubɛiden ay mazal ur ten-id-ufin. |
| Imẓerbeḍḍa gan tigrawin deg Facebook |  sṭerṭiḥen din am lmal deg uddaynin-nni ameqran. Wa ad ijeɛɛu |  wa ad yesrugmut |  wa ad yesqaqay |  wa ad yesseglaf |  sakkin ad ttaḍsan akk |  yal yiwen yeɛjeb-it usuɣu n wayeḍ |  neɣ ad ttemyergamen imi rregmat ɣer-sen maci d lɛib. |
| Imi ggten yismal web ɣef yal d asentel |  tekkayeɣ dima ɣef tqeffalt uɣal ɣer deffir m ara d-afeɣ iman-iw di kra n usebter yesɛan adellel i d-iteffɣen. Ttruḥuɣ dɣa ɣer usebter nniḍen kan n zzat i d-yessumer Google wissen ad d-ɣliɣ i kra nniḍen ur nessefqaɛ akken. |
| Amazellaw agriwlan uqrib akk ɣer umazellaw-nneɣ n Ubrid n Walim netta d amazellaw n Nedṛumida. Amazellaw-a yebɛed fell-aɣ s sin n yimelyunen n yiseggasen n tafat. Aweggir-nnes alemmas d yiɣallen-nnes igriwlanen malen-d ɣer-neɣ s teɣmert n mraw semmus n tfesniwin. |
| ASSEMTER I YIMAWLAN: lemmer ad sqedcen warraw-nwen TATOEBA akken ad zerwen tutlayin |  ttxil-wen |  sfeqdet awalen ur tbeɣɣum ad ten-ɣren - ur ttsetḥit! Ur tezmirem ad d-tessugnem awalen icemten ay ttɛemmiden ad ten-sqedcen da imi ay ttwalin dakken tutlayt d tutlayt. |
| Ferhat Mehenni |  amalway n umussu amẓerbeḍḍu |  yebɣa ad d-yessebded awanak uxṣir deg yiwet n temnaḍt ixuṣṣen tiɣbula |  yernu s tallalt n wakk icenga n Lezzayer. Maɣef kan ur d-yessebdad ara awanak-a deg kra n temnaḍt deg Kanada |  anda ay ddren aṭas seg yineḍfaren-nnes? |
| Naqal zik |  imẓerbeḍḍa llan d iremmaɣen kan deg Internet. Imir-a |  s yiznan-nsen n tuggza ed teɣra i yimeddukal-nsen akken ad rkin medden deg ubrid |  qqlen d iremmaɣen ula deg tilawt. D acu kan |  aya ur yessewham ara imi ula d aɣella-nsen iger-d tiɣri i urfad n yimrigen. |
| S usseɣnew n Tkadimit Tazzayrit n Tutlayt Tamaziɣt |  teqqel-as tadimt i txuzziḍt n yimẓerbeḍḍa ay yebɣan ad d-snulfun tutlayt i yiman-nsen. Nitni werǧin sɛin tutlayt |  maca asmi ay walan tebda tetteflali-d tutlayt tamaziɣt |  bdan sxurruḍen dakken ula d nitni sɛan tutlayt. |
| Amsatwil-nni n yimẓerbeḍḍa tettergigi tjeḥniḍt-nnes yal tikkelt aydeg ara d-yas ɣer Lezzayer Tamaneɣt. ɛni wissen d acu ay yuggad ad as-t-geɣ. Ma d nekk |  melmi ay iyi-yehwa ttedduɣ ɣer tuddar n Tmurt n Leqbayel |  ttadfeɣ taddart ay iyi-yehwan yernu ur ttaggadeɣ seg yiwen. |
| Neẓra dakken tagrawt tamẓerbeḍḍut la tetteg taḥemla n ucemmet deg yiẓeḍwan inmettiyen mgal kra n yimdanen ay tt-yexḍan. D ayyuren aya seg wasmi ay la d-njemmeɛ inzaten akken ad neccetki fell-asen deg teɣdemt. Wid ay yesmendgen times deg tḥemla-a ulac akk sanda ara rewlen. |
| Aṭas seg yimẓerbeḍḍa-nni ay yettekkan deg tḥemla n ucemmet ed tirawt n yiznan n tuggza ttwassnen s yismawen-nsen n tidet deg yiẓeḍwan inmettiyen. D aya ay aɣ-yeǧǧan ad neccetki fell-asen ɣer yimeẓla n tɣellist ay yebdan yagi tasestant-nnes akken ad ten-id-tezzuɣer ɣer tnefrut. |
| Ma ur telliḍ d yiwen seg-sen |  ur telliḍ d acemma ɣer-sen |  yerna i wakken ad tiliḍ d yiwen seg-sen |  yessefk ad tiliḍ tluleḍ-d deg tmurt-nsen yerna tgiḍ am nitni |  yerna yessefk daɣen ad tettxemmimeḍ am nitni. Skud temgerradeḍ fell-asen |  ad k-keṛhen war tasebba. Nitni d imsiriyen. |
| Igḍaḍ axxam-nsen d tiẓgi |  iselman axxam-nsen d asif |  tizizwa axxam-nsent d tijejjigin |  ma d igerdan imeẓyanen axxam-nsen d Ccinwa. Nḥemmel tamurt-nneɣ seg wasmi ara nili d imeẓyanen |  swaswa am yegḍaḍ ay iḥemmlen tiẓgi |  iselman ay iḥemmlen asif akked tzizwa ay iḥemmlen tijejjigin. |
| Bɣan ad awyen akal |  maca llan yemdanen deg wakal-nni. Bɣan ad hennin seg yemdanen-nni |  dɣa semman-asen iweḥciyen. Ma ifat semman-asen iweḥciyen |  imdanen-nni ur mazal ad ttwaḥesben d imdanen. Dɣa yeqqel ussenger-nsen iḥell |  yerna akka ara yeqqel wakal n kra n ljens d ayla n ljens niḍen. |
| Mi ara iwali kra n temsal ɛeddant tilas |  lbaṭel yessemɣi-d acciwen |  tamuḥeqranit txeddem i tebɣa |  imir-nni kan ad yeɛnu adeg anda ara yeqqim ala iman-is |  ad d-yerfed imru ad d-yernu taferkit tamellalt |  ad yebdu ad yessuru iḥulfan-is fell-as |  s usefru ara yaru deg tutlayt-nni iwumi immečč lheqq. |
| Neṛja armi d asmi ay d-yewweḍ uɣella n tegrawt tamẓerbeḍḍut |  s usenfar-nnes n ubeḍḍu |  akken ad nẓer d acu-tt tutlayt ay nessawal. S waya |  yessefk ad nzelli neɣ ad nesserɣ akk idlisen n tesnilest ay d-uran Chaker |  Nait-Zerrad |  Basset |  Haddadou ed waṭas n yimazzagen niḍen. Tanemmirt a imẓerbeḍḍa. |
| Nekni s weɣref n Yiwunak-Yedduklen |  akken ad teblel ugar tdukli-nneɣ |  u ad nesbedd taɣdemt |  u ad nreṣṣit talwit tagensut |  u ad nessijhed timḥaddit tucrikt d liser amatu |  u ad neḍmen lfayda i ɣ-d-tewwi tlelli i nekni d wid ara d-iḍefren deffir-neɣ |  atan ad d-nesyi Tamendawt-a i Iwunak n Marikan Yedduklen. |
| Imẓerbeḍḍa ay aɣ-d-yuznen iznan n tuggza ɣilen dakken mazal tallit-nni aydeg ara yazen yiwen izen aliktṛunan i wayeḍ yernu yiwen ur yezmir ad iẓer seg wansi ay t-id-yuzen. Ass-a tella temsulta tussnant yernu zemren ad d-jebden s kra n unejrim ara yesqedcen aselkim-nnes akken ad yazen yes-s iznan n tuggza. |
| Inglusaksunen mačči kan d akal-ik ara awin. Ad k-ṭṭfen daɣen d akli |  dɣa mara temmteḍ ad sersen iɣsan-ik di kra usalay u ad k-id-gelmen deg idlisen umezruy ara arun am akken d aweḥci i tuɣ telliḍ. Syin ad rnun ad gen fell-ak isura iwakken ad d-beyynen amek akken telliḍ tcemteḍ d wamek fazen isaṭṭen-nsen deg tebɣest. |
| Imgura ay ttnaɣen Yiwunak Yeddukklen deg Asya ur sɛin assaɣ akked tugdut neɣ assenger n tremmiɣt. Wi d imgura ikelsertiyen ayyes Iwunak Yeddukklen bɣan ad awyen apitṛul n Wegmuḍ Alemmas |  Quqaz ed Asya Talemmast |  yerna bɣan daɣen ad ḥeṛsen timura ay ijehden am Rusya |  Ccinwa ed Lhend i wakken ur tetterni tezmert-nsent. |
| Yemma-s mi ara tetturar d mmi-s netta mazal-it iteṭteḍ tabbuct |  tecennu-as akka: Ad nǧelleb tiǧellibin Am wuccen ɣer tebḥirin Ad d-nawi tiqlalacin I yemma-s |  ad d-tfek tiɛuɛɛucin ɛeslama seg xuxuc Taqbuct n ɛuɛɛuc Sbaḥ lxir seg yiḍes Ay ajeǧǧig n yifires Sbaḥ lxir a leɛyun n ṭṭir Ṭṭbeq n uzanǧar iwimi yekkes uqedmir . |
| Ata yuli-d ṣṣut n lbuq |  dɣa akken i s-yesla wegdud |  isuɣ asuɣu meqqren |  ihi u ad yedrem ugadir ɣef tikelt. Din din |  mmɣen wat Israyil ɣef temdint |  yal wa ɣer zzat |  armi tt-ṭṭfen. Imir |  akken ad ten-aznen s Amaɣlal |  ssnegren argaz tameṭṭut |  imecṭaḥ mɣaren |  izgaren |  akraren d yeɣyal : meḥsub ayen akk tuɣ yettidiren deg temdint. |
| Qbel ciṭuḥ |  iḍ-a |  yewweḍ-iyi-d usiwel d imreyyes maḍi sɣur usinatur McCain. Asinatur McCain aṭas i iwet |  i yesɛedda deg tawayt-a n tefranin. Iwet ugar yerna yesɛedda daɣen aṭas ɣef tmurt i iḥemmel. Yeqbel ad isebbel ɣef Marikan ayen ur d-tessugun tuget deg-neɣ. S wayen i d-yefka umqeddem-a abɣas ur yezdiɣ ṭṭmeɛ |  i nuɣal ngerrez. |
| Allo? Yemma? D acu a Sami. Yella baba deg uxxam? Ih. Zemreɣ ad mmeslayeɣ yid-s? Atan la yessucuf. Yemma? D acu a aɛziz-iw? Bɣiɣ ad kem-id-xebbreɣ s kra. D acu-t? Ilaq ad tiliḍ tzemreḍ i tmesliwt-is |  akk-a? Ih |  d acu-t? Yeḍra kra yessexlaɛen i Farid. D acu?! A ya? Allo? Mazal-iken din? Ahya a Ṛebbi! A ya ... suref-iyi a ya |  ttxilem suref-iyi. |
| Ɣilen yimẓerbeḍḍa dakken ma regmen yiwen neɣ sin seg yimeɣnasen n tmaziɣt |  d Amussu Adelsan Amaziɣ s timmad-nnes ara iḥebsen. Imẓerbeḍḍa d leɛṛuṛ |  inaw-nsen d lɛaṛ |  tigawt-nsen d lɛaṛ |  amahil-nsen d lɛaṛ yernu ur tettɛeḍḍil ara ad teɣli tegrawt-nsen |  ad tt-yessired zzman am uxunnis n yiẓẓan mi ara t-tessired tḥemmalt n waman deg wass n ugeffur. |
| Ad shersen akal |  ad ẓẓɛen seg-s iserwen |  ad d-sbedden anhil amsiri ara iqeren iserwen ay d-yeqqimen |  ad as-semmin anhil amegday |  yernu ad ɣsen ad ddren deg talwit deg wakud aydeg ara kemmlen ad snegzaren iserwen yernu ad asen-semmin i wakk wid ay yezban iremmaɣen |  akken yebɣu yili webrid n wezbu-nsen. D ta ay d tilawt torwellit aydeg ddren kra n yiɣerfan. |
| Aɣrab n ubeḍḍu amsiri deg Falesṭin yesɛa |  ɣef leḥsab-inu |  nnfeɛ atakti. Ad d-yili weɣrab-a d agadir lemmer ad d-yenker wemgaru n ussenger yessexlaɛen kra n wass ɣef lǧal n uṭṭerḍeq n wurfan n Yifalesṭiniyen ay yeddren acḥal n tmerwin n yiseggasen ddaw lbaṭel ay ten-imeḥqen. Ad yili wemgaru-a d ssebba i ussedrem d tuẓẓɛa n Yifalesṭiniyen ineggura seg Ugemmaḍ Utrim |  anect bɣun ilin. |
| Ur d tamurt-nwen kan ay yellan deg umaḍal. Lemmer ad teddum s agafa |  ad tafem Kanada |  Agaraw Aṛkti ed Rusya. Lemmer ad teddim s anẓul |  ad tafem Miksik |  Guatemala ed wakk Tamrikt arma d Taṛjentint n ed Cili. Deg wegmuḍ |  ad tafem Tuṛuft ed Tefriqt s wakk iɣlanen-nsent. Deg utaram |  ad tafem Asya s wakk iɣerfan ed yidelsan-nnes. Kenwi d aḥric kan seg umaḍal. Ur d amaḍal ay yellan d aḥric seg-wen. |
| D iserdasen i nella di Fransa |  yerna d iɣermanen. D ssebba-iḍen iss ara nzuxx |  imi d iɣermanen ! Meḥsub igellilen ilaq-asen ad ɛassen u ad ḥadren ɣef yimeṛkantiyen inezmaren ur nesɛi ara xedmen. Yessefk ad aɣen awal i temsawit isuḍaf i igedlen nadam ddaw tqneṭyar ama i imeṛkantiyen neɣ i igellilen am akken i sen-teqḍeɛ daɣ tuttra deg iberdan d tukerḍa n weɣrum. D aḥric si lxir d-tewwi Tegrawla. |
| Imi ay bɣan yimẓerbeḍḍa ad rren tantala taqbaylit d tutlayt i yiman-nnes |  ttxil-wen |  init-iyi-d: Amek ara ḥesben tasaḥlit? D tantala taqbaylit neɣ d tutlayt i yiman-nnes? Ferhat Mehenni |  s tmussni-nnes talqayant |  yezmer ad yegzu tasaḥlit? I ma ur tt-yegzi ara |  ad tt-yeḥseb d tutlayt neɣ d tantala kan n teqbaylit? Imẓerbeḍḍa werǧin ad d-rren ɣef waya. Ttgugumen yal tikkelt aydeg ara asen-nini ma yettakf-d yizirekki tamemt. |
| Ulac ccek dakken yal argaz yesɛa tameṭṭut ay t-iwatan swaswa akken ad tt-yaɣ yernu akka daɣ ay yella lḥal ed yal tameṭṭut. D acu kan |  mi ara nẓer dakken amdan yezmer ad yessen kra kan n timaḍ n yimdanen |  yernu seg gar timaḍ-a |  ur ttawḍen ara mraw n yimdanen wukud ara yecrek lbaḍna |  yernu mi ara d-nemmekti dakken d imelyunen n yimdanen ay izedɣen deg umaḍal |  ulac ccek dakken |  seg wasmi ay d-yettwaxleq umaḍal |  werǧin yemlal-d kra n urgaz ed tmeṭṭut ay t-iwatan. |
| Imẓerbeḍḍa teḍra-asen am yimeẓrislamen-nni yessexlaḍen iẓẓan ed tamemt. Imeẓrislamen ssnen kan taɛṛabt yernu xḍan akk tamaziɣt |  maca mi ara bɣun ad gren iman-nsen deg tesnilest |  ttinin-aɣ-d: Arut tamaziɣt s ugemmay aɛṛab. Imẓerbeḍḍa |  ur yettgen ara daɣ amgerrad gar yiẓẓan ed tamemt |  imi ay sɛan asenfar asertan d afuḥan |  ɣunfan-t akk medden |  snulfan-d tutlayt taqbaylit akken ad kellxen i kra n yibeṛhac |  yernu nekṛen tella tutlayt tamaziɣt. Imẓerbeḍḍa ed yimeẓrislamen ttetten seg yiwet n tbaqit: tin n tamemt ed yiẓẓan. |
